<script>
    /* Added Deferred and the code below to fix menu render problem */
    $("#menu1").kendoMenu();

    $(document).click(function (event) {
        var isMenuClick = false;
        if (!($(event.target).hasClass("menuheader") || $(event.target).hasClass("menuheaderrollover") || $(event.target).hasClass("k-icon k-i-arrow-s")))
        {
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; 8; i++)
            {
                if ($(event.target).closest('#menudropdown' + i).length)
                {
                    isMenuClick = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!isMenuClick)
            {
                hideopendropdowns(8);
            }
        }
    });
</script>

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;

                $('#dvGridSettings__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

            cache: false,
            async: false,

            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'PayrollDeductionManagementDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });

                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();

                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___PayrollDeductionManagementDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("PayrollDeductionManagementDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView() {
        var gridName = 'PayrollDeductionManagementDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___PayrollDeductionManagementDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_PayrollDeductionManagementDataView');

        if (parseBool("True")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "PayrollDeductionManagementDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_PayrollDeductionManagementDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $('#UnselectAll__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divPayrollDeductionManagementDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

<script type="text/javascript">

    $("#btnPreviewNetPay__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").click(function () {

        var grid = $("#PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        var data = { deductionId: selectedRowIds };

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/GetDataForPreviewNetPayByDeduction',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {
                    window.location.href = "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/PreviewNetPayDeduction" + "?id=" + result.Data;
                }
            }
        });
    });

    $("#btnRolloverDeduction__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").click(function () {

        var selectedRowIds = GetGridSelectedId("PayrollDeductionManagementDataView");
        if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/Rollover" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject('popupwindowRolloverDeduction')
                                  .SetContent(options)
                                  .SetHeight('20%')
                                  .SetWidth(550)
                                  .SetIsModal(true)
                                  .SetTitle('Rollover Deductions')

        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    });

    $("#btnSystemDeduction__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").click(function () {
        var kendoWindow = $("#popupwindowSystemDeduction").kendoWindow({
            content: { url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/SystemDeduction" },
            title: "Create System Deduction",
            modal: true,
            refresh: function (e) { e.sender.center(); }
        });

        kendoWindow.data("kendoWindow").setOptions({
            width: 500,
            height: 480
        });

        kendoWindow.data("kendoWindow").center().open();
    });

    $("#btnCopyDeduction__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").click(function () {

        var grid = $("#PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm", "Are you sure you want to copy the selected deduction?", function () {
            window.location.href = "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/CopyDeduction" + "/" + selectedRowIds;
        });

    });

    function IsEnabled() {
        var grid = $("#PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        var gridData = grid.dataSource.data();

        for (var i = 0; i &lt; gridData.length; i++) {
            if (gridData[i].Id == selectedRowIds) {
                var EnabledStatus = gridData[i].EnabledStatus;

                if (EnabledStatus) {
                    return true;
                }
                break;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    function EnableDisableDeductions(operation) {
        var selectedRowIds = $("#divPayrollDeductionManagementDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
        var data = { aptaDataViewSelection: selectedRowIds };
        var url = operation == "Enable" ? '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/EnableDeduction' : '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/DisableDeduction';
        var title = operation == "Enable" ? 'Enable Deduction' : 'Disable Deduction';
        $.ajax({
            url: url,
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            type: "POST",
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {
                if (result.Success) {
                    if (result.HasException)
                        showExceptionpopup(selectedRowIds);
                    else {
                        StartJobQueueNotifications();
                        ShowAjaxMessage((operation == "Enable" ? 'Enable Deduction' : 'Disable Deduction') + " - " + "Your process has been started and is now in the job queue. You will be notified when it is complete.", "success");
                    }
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                    if (result.HasException)
                        showExceptionpopup(selectedRowIds);
                }
            }
        });

    }

    $("#btnEnableDeduction__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").click(function () {
        var grid = $("#PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!$("#divPayrollDeductionManagementDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation."))
            return;
        ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm", "Are you sure you want to enable the selected deduction(s)?", function () {
            EnableDisableDeductions('Enable');
        });
    });

    $("#btnDisableDeduction__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").click(function () {
        var grid = $("#PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!$("#divPayrollDeductionManagementDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation."))
            return;

        ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm", "Are you sure you want to disable the selected deduction(s)?", function () {
            EnableDisableDeductions('Disable');
        });
    });

    $("#btnDelete__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        var gridData = grid.dataSource.data();
        var deductionStatus;
        var deductionEnableStatus;
        for (var i = 0; i &lt; gridData.length; i++) {
            if (gridData[i].Id == selectedRowIds) {
                deductionStatus = gridData[i].ActiveStatus;
                deductionEnableStatus = gridData[i].EnabledStatusString;
                break;
            }
        }
        if (deductionStatus == 'Active' || deductionEnableStatus == 'Enabled') {
            ShowOkDialog("Delete Deduction", "Only disabled inactive deduction can be deleted.");
        }
        else {
            ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected deduction?", DeleteDeduction);
        }

    });

    function DeleteDeduction() {
        var grid = $("#PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/DeleteDeduction" + "/" + selectedRowIds;
    }

    $("#btnAdd__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").click(function () {
        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/Create";
    });

    $("#btnEdit__PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").click(function () {

        var grid = $("#PayrollDeductionManagementDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        //post the selected items and the selected value
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/MultipleEdit",
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (returnData) {
                if (returnData) {
                    window.location.href = "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/Details/" + returnData.DeductionId;
                }
            }
        });

    });
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).click(function (event) {

            if (event.target.id == "btnMoreButtons" || event.target.parentNode.id == "btnMoreButtons") {
                event.preventDefault();
                showHideMoreButtons();
            }
            else {
                if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    document.getElementById("dvMoreButtons").style.display = "none";
                }
            }
            if (event.target.classList.contains('btnDetailMoreButtons') || (event.target.parentNode != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList.contains("btnDetailMoreButtons"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var id = event.target.id;
                if (event.target.id == "") {
                    id = event.target.parentNode.id;
                }
                showHideDetailMoreButtons(id);
            }
            else {
                if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                        $(this).css('display', 'none');
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                ShowMoreMenu();
            }
            if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).css('display') != 'none') {
                        ShowDetailMoreMenu(this.id);
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            ResetDivMoreButtonOnResize();
        });

        var _jobQueueNotificationTimer;

        function StartJobQueueNotifications() {
            if (_jobQueueNotificationTimer == null)
                CheckJobQueueNotifications('/QAAutom/Home/CheckJobQueueStatus');
        }

        function DismissJobQueueNotification(jobQueueID) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                async: false,
                data: { jobQueueID: jobQueueID },
                dataType: "json",
                url: '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/DismissJobQueueStatus',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Message != "") {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().ShowJobQueueNotification(result.TempData, result.Message)
                    } else {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().hide();
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    </script>


<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        FINSUI.FINSUIElement.setAptaFundBaseURL("/QAAutom/controller/action", true);
        

        if ('' == "Detail") {
            doStickyButtons();
        }
        registerFINSComboBoxEvents();
        $("body").find("input, textarea, select, span[role=listbox]").filter(":visible:not([disabled]):not([readonly]):not([tabindex=-1]):first").focus();

    });

    function doStickyButtons() {
        var sticky_button_offset_top = $('#menuhr').offset().top;

        // our function that decides weather the navigation bar should have "fixed" css position or not.
        var sticky_button_navigation = function () {
            var scroll_top = $(window).scrollTop(); // our current vertical position from the top
            var screenwidth = $(window).width();
            var buttonswidth = $('#actionbuttons').width();
            var buttonsheight = $('#actionbuttons').height();

            // if we've scrolled more than the navigation, change its position to fixed to stick to top,
            // otherwise change it back to relative
            if (scroll_top &gt; sticky_button_offset_top) {
                $('#menuhr').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 0, 'left': 40, 'z-index': 11, 'width': (screenwidth - 80) });
                $('#actionbuttons').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 10, 'right': 48, 'z-index': 12, 'width': buttonswidth });
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').css({ 'height': buttonsheight });
            } else {
                $('#menuhr').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttons').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').removeAttr('style');
            }
        };

        // run our function on load
        sticky_button_navigation();

        // and run it again every time you scroll
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            sticky_button_navigation();
        });
    }

    
    function registerFINSComboBoxEvents() {
        $('.FINSComboBox').each(function () {
            var kendoCombo = $(this).data("kendoComboBox");
            if (kendoCombo != null) {

                kendoCombo.bind("select", function (e) {
                    if (e.item != null) {
                        var dataItem = this.dataItem(e.item.index());
                        if (dataItem.Value == -999) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                }
               );

            }
        });
    }
